<p>RULES OF OPERATION OF THE OREKA.VN E-COMMERCE SERVICES WEBSITE</p>
<p>Originating from the desire to reduce carbon emissions (CO2 emissions) for a greener earth. We aim to create an effective way to sell used items that are still good and useful to consumers. By effectively buying and selling items that are no longer needed, we can reduce the need to produce new items, which is how we reduce carbon emissions on earth through Oreka.vn.</p>
<p>I. General principles<br>The Oreka.vn e-commerce website is operated and managed by Oreka Vietnam Company Limited (the Company). Members on the Website are merchants, organizations, and individuals with legal commercial activities officially recognized by Oreka.vn and are allowed to use services provided by Oreka.vn and related parties.</p>
<p>This principle applies to members who register to use and participate in providing products and services on Oreka.vn.</p>
<p>Merchants, organizations, and individuals participating in transactions at Oreka.vn freely negotiate on the basis of respecting the rights and legitimate interests of the parties participating in the purchase and sale of products and services through contracts, not contrary to the provisions of law.</p>
<p>Information about merchants, organizations, and individuals who are members on Oreka.vn must be transparent and accurate.</p>
<p>Products and services participating in transactions on Oreka.vn must fully comply with the provisions of relevant laws, not falling under the cases of prohibited business or advertising according to the provisions of law.</p>
<p>The purchase and sale of goods and provision of services via Oreka.vn must be carried out publicly, transparently, and ensure the rights of consumers.</p>
<p>All contents in this Regulation must comply with the current legal system of Vietnam. When participating in Oreka.vn, members must understand their legal responsibilities under the current laws of Vietnam and commit to comply with the contents of the Oreka.vn Regulations.</p>
<p>II. General provisions<br>Domain name of E-commerce Website:</p>
<p>The Oreka.vn e-commerce website is developed by Oreka Vietnam Company Limited with the name: Oreka.vn (hereinafter referred to as: "Oreka.vn Website").</p>
<p>Oreka Vietnam Company Limited was established and operates under the Business Registration Certificate No. 0109460213 issued by the Hanoi Department of Planning and Investment for the first time on December 17, 2020.</p>
<p>General definition:</p>
<p>Seller: is an individual, trader, or organization with legal business and commercial activities that Oreka.vn agrees to allow to use the services provided by the Oreka.vn Website and related parties. Through Oreka.vn, â€œSellerâ€ creates a booth to display, introduce, and perform other activities to provide Products to Buyers.</p>
<p>Buyer/Buyer: is an individual or trader who registers an account on the Oreka.vn Website to purchase products and services from the Seller on Oreka.vn.</p>
<p>Product: is the goods that the Seller is trading and providing on the Oreka.vn Website.</p>
<p>Oreka.vn Website Management Board or Management Board: is the group that develops and operates the Oreka.vn e-commerce website project, authorized by Oreka Vietnam Company Limited to be responsible for and manage related issues.</p>
<p>Members: including both Sellers and Buyers</p>
<p>Members must register to initially declare relevant personal information, be officially recognized by the Oreka.vn Management Board and be allowed to use the service.</p>
<p>When a member registers as a member of the Oreka.vn Website, the member understands that:</p>
<p>+ Members can create their own personal account for use.</p>
<p>+ Members can receive product information from Sellers</p>
<p>The content of this Regulation complies with current regulations of Vietnam. When participating in the Oreka.vn Website, members must understand their legal responsibilities under current Vietnamese laws and commit to properly implementing the contents of the Regulations of the Oreka.vn Website.</p>
<p>III. Transaction process<br>1. Purchase process on Oreka.vn<br>When there is a need to buy a product on Oreka.vn, the buyer should follow these steps:</p>
<p>Step 1: Register and Log in to the buyer account on Oreka.vn</p>
<p>Step 2: The buyer searches for and references product information, prices, images and information, and the booth of the Seller that the buyer is interested in.</p>
<p>Step 3: The buyer references specific information about the model, details, comments of the product, conditions and support policies of the Seller of the product that the Buyer is interested in buying (can refer to similar items of other Sellers on the Oreka.vn Website).</p>
<p>Step 4: Based on the reference information from the Product Seller, the Buyer can make a decision to order online by clicking on "Buy Now" or "Add to Cart" to order multiple products.</p>
<p>Step 5: The buyer checks the order information before paying.</p>
<p>Step 6: Select â€œPaymentâ€ and choose the desired payment method.</p>
<p>If the buyer chooses the online payment method, the system will transfer to the Payment Gateway interface, the buyer enters information or makes payment.</p>
<p>The system notifies that the order is successful.</p>
<p>Step 7: The Buyer receives the Product from the shipping unit;</p>
<p>Step 8: The Buyer writes feedback and sends questions and complaints to the Seller via the website Oreka.vn (if any). The Seller will directly resolve the complaint and questions for the buyer if the error is related to the Seller's product (if any)</p>
<p>2. Sales process on Oreka.vn<br>Step 1: User creates an account and logs in on Oreka.vn.</p>
<p>Step 2: Seller updates personal/business information and verifies by providing personal ID/CCCD/Passport information or business registration certificate.</p>
<p>Step 3: Using this account, after logging in, Seller proceeds to post Product information and Seller information, complying with posting regulations.</p>
<p>Step 4: In case the seller has not been verified, when choosing to post a product, there will be a notification from the system to update seller information.</p>
<p>In case the seller has been verified, the product after posting will be displayed in the corresponding category.</p>
<p>Step 5: After the Buyer successfully places an order, the Seller can check the order in the "Sale Order" section.</p>
<p>Step 6: The seller delivers the goods to the linked shipping unit for delivery to the Buyer, based on the Buyer information provided in the order on Oreka.vn.</p>
<p>Step 7: The seller tracks the order and/or handles the return and exchange procedures and Buyer complaints (if any).</p>
<p>Step 8: The seller evaluates the buyer's transaction experience.</p>
<p>3. Order confirmation/cancellation process<br>Step 1: The buyer places an order and pays, the system notifies that the order has been successfully placed</p>
<p>Step 2: The seller receives the buyer's order information and confirms the order in the seller's account.</p>
<p>Step 3: The seller prepares the goods and packages them for shipping.</p>
<p>Step 4: The shipping party receives the goods at the seller's address and delivers them to the buyer.</p>
<p>In case the seller cancels the order, Oreka will notify the buyer and make a refund if the buyer has paid online.</p>
<p>Refund processing is done by Oreka within 1-3 business days. The time it takes for the Buyer to receive the refund depends on the processing procedure of the bank the Buyer used to make the payment.</p>
<p>4. Delivery and shipping policy<br>After the Buyer places an order, the seller checks and confirms the Buyer's order. The system automatically transfers the order to the shipping service.</p>
<p>The seller is responsible for preparing the product and packaging it according to standards for delivery to the shipping company. The shipping unit will receive the goods from the seller and deliver them to the buyer.</p>
<p>Shipping costs are specified for each product, the seller or the buyer bears the shipping costs.</p>
<p>Delivery costs and other surcharges (if any) depend on a number of factors such as bulky goods, heavy goods, or the distance from the seller to the buyer, and product packaging requirements. For products that incur these costs/surcharges, the seller is responsible for providing clear information in the product description (size, weight) for Oreka to update in the order with the shipping company.</p>
<p>These shipping costs are calculated (estimated) by the system and notified at the time the Buyer places an order and before confirming payment. The cost ranges from 20,000 VND - 50,000 VND/order.</p>
<p>Estimated delivery time is within 3-5 days depending on the area. If there is any change, the seller is responsible for notifying the shipping unit and the Buyer of the delayed delivery time.</p>
<p>The seller is fully responsible for resolving complaints with Buyers regarding late delivery to the shipping unit, regarding packaging specifications affecting product quality.</p>
<p>In case the product is lost or cannot be delivered during the shipping process, the seller and Oreka.vn need to coordinate to resolve the problem.</p>
<p>Oreka.vn is also responsible for supporting information to the Seller or the purchasing Buyer when requested so that the parties can negotiate with each other to resolve the problem.</p>
<p>5. Warranty policy<br>Products sold by Sellers on the Oreka.vn Website are committed to the correct product quality as declared in each product by the Seller.</p>
<p>Due to the nature of the products on Oreka being used products, the warranty policy (if any) will be stated in the product description. The Seller is responsible for describing in detail the product warranty policy (if any) when posting for sale.</p>
<p>For the Seller's products, Oreka.vn is not the direct supplier but only a trade promotion support unit. Therefore, Oreka.vn recommends that buyers check each type of product and the warranty policy for that product before placing an order.</p>
<p>Oreka.vn will only provide information within its capacity in the event that the Seller fails to properly fulfill its product warranty obligations (if any) to the Buyer and/or a related dispute arises when requested for support by either party.</p>
<p>Email for support information: <a href="mailto:hotro@oreka.vn">hotro@oreka.vn</a>.</p>
<p>6. Return Policy<br>Due to the nature of the products on Oreka being used products, the return policy (if any) will be stated in the product description. The seller is responsible for describing the product's return policy in detail (if any) when posting for sale.</p>
<p>For the Seller's products, Oreka.vn is not the direct supplier but only a trade promotion support unit. Therefore, Oreka.vn is not responsible for returning products to Buyers. We recommend that buyers check each product type and the return policy for that product before placing an order.</p>
<p>To limit the occurrence of returns, the Seller is responsible for checking the quality of the product and the package. In case of any complaints arising from the buyer, the Seller is responsible for resolving the complaint or dispute</p>
<p>The two parties, the Buyer and the Seller, will discuss and agree with each other in case of a return. Oreka.vn will only provide information support within its capacity in the event that the Seller fails to properly fulfill its obligation to return the product to the Buyer and/or a related dispute arises when requested for support by either party.</p>
<p>Email for receiving support information: hotro@oreka.vn.</p>
<p>7. Dispute and complaint resolution process<br>Oreka.vn and the Seller are responsible for receiving and handling complaints from buyers related to transactions on the Oreka.vn Website.</p>
<p>Buyers have the right to submit complaints about product quality, services not matching the description, payment information being disclosed causing damage to them to the Oreka.vn Management Board. After receiving these reflections, we will verify the information, if true as reflected, we will propose a solution for both parties including the Buyer and the Seller.</p>
<p>Buyers send complaints to the following address:</p>
<p>- Oreka Vietnam Co., Ltd.</p>
<p>- Address: B2-25 Vinhomes Gardenia, Ham Nghi Street, Cau Dien, Nam Tu Liem, Hanoi</p>
<p>- Email: hotro@oreka.vn - Phone: 0904433126</p>
<p>Steps to resolve disputes and complaints:</p>
<p>Step 1: The Company's Buyer Service Department will receive Buyer complaints. These Departments will proactively resolve them quickly and immediately respond to the results of resolving complaints based on the Company's published policies.</p>
<p>Step 2: In cases that are complicated or not specified in the Company's published policies, the Buyer Service Department will commit to a response time for Buyers.<br>The time to process Buyer complaints is 24 - 72 hours</p>
<p>Step 3: Transfer the results of the complaint resolution to relevant departments for implementation and call to confirm with the Buyer that the complaint has been resolved.</p>
<p>Oreka.vn respects and strictly implements the provisions of law on protecting the rights of Buyers. Therefore, it is recommended that Sellers on the platform provide complete, accurate, honest and detailed information related to products and services. Any fraudulent or deceptive business behavior is condemned and must be held fully responsible before the law.</p>
<p>We publicly disclose the mechanism for resolving disputes arising during transactions on the Oreka.vn Website. When Buyers purchase goods or services that have conflicts with the Seller or are harmed by their legitimate interests, Oreka.vn will provide the Buyer with the Seller's registration information immediately after receiving the Buyer's request.</p>
<p>Oreka.vn publicly discloses the mechanism and process for resolving disputes to related parties: resolving disputes according to a unified agreement exchange mechanism, related parties will follow the indirect exchange process via phone, confirmation via email, if still unable to reach an agreement, it will be resolved through a direct meeting to specify the problem, thoroughly resolving the conflict between the parties in the most beneficial way.</p>
<p>The parties including the Seller, the Buyer and Oreka.vn will have to play a responsible role in actively resolving the problem. For the Seller, it is necessary to provide documents certifying information related to the incident that is causing the conflict for the Buyer. Oreka.vn will be responsible for the arbitration to listen and receive information from the Buyer (in specific cases, we will: require the Buyer to be responsible for providing accurate invisible and tangible information about the arising conflict that needs to be resolved and that the Buyer has seen himself damaged) and the Seller, then proceed to review and clarify, analyze which party is at fault. Get opinions on the agreement on the level of compensation from both parties and end the dispute in the most satisfactory way.</p>
<p>In case it is proven that the fault belongs to the Seller, Oreka.vn will take measures to warn, request a refund of all costs that the Buyer has had to spend to own that product/service or must exchange the product, service with the quality that the Seller announced on Oreka.vn. If the Seller re-offends, Oreka.vn will terminate and remove all information of that Seller on Oreka.vn.</p>
<p>If through the form of agreement, the conflict arising from the transaction cannot be resolved, Oreka.vn will request one of the two parties to seek the intervention of a competent legal agency to ensure the legitimate interests of the parties, especially for the Buyers.</p>
<p>IV. Payment process<br>1. Payment process for Buyers purchasing on Oreka.vn</p>
<p>In addition to the payment method upon receipt of goods, Oreka is implementing Internet Banking payment, international payment cards, ATM card payment via the Ngan Luong payment gateway. Therefore, Buyers can refer to the payment process below when purchasing:</p>
<p>Step 1: Buyers learn about information about products/services posted on the Website;<br>Step 2: Buyers place orders, provide necessary information<br>Â· Step 3: Buyers choose payment methods accepted on the website: Payment by ATM card via the AlePay gateway, Internet Banking payment, payment by international payment cards Visa, Master Card, JCB<br>Â· Step 4: The system redirects Buyers to make safe payments at the payment gateway interface. Buyers enter information to complete payment.<br>Â· Step 5: The Oreka.vn system notifies that the order is successful.<br>Â· Step 6: Seller confirms order and prepares goods for delivery to the shipping unit<br>Â· Step 7: Buyer receives goods from the shipping unit.</p>
<p>In case the buyer's order is canceled after paying online, the refund process is as follows:</p>
<p>- Order confirmed cancellation</p>
<p>- Oreka sends a request to the payment gateway that the buyer used for a refund.</p>
<p>- Buyer receives 100% refund</p>
<p>- Buyer does not incur any costs for canceling the order (if the order is canceled by the seller)</p>
<p>2. Payment process between Seller and Oreka.vn</p>
<p>Oreka.vn charges the Seller a commission based on the orders sold through the Platform.</p>
<p>Commission fee is calculated by a commission rate calculated on each product sold on the Website multiplied by the listed selling price of that Product</p>
<p>Sales fee: 9.9% of the product value (7.9% sales fee and 2% transaction processing fee)</p>
<p>The two parties will check and compare the data of successful transactions when the Seller sends a payment request to Oreka, specifically as follows:</p>
<p>- Check data: .</p>
<p>The Seller will log in to the management account to track revenue statistics.</p>
<p>- When wanting to withdraw money, the Seller sends a withdrawal request to Oreka in the "My Money" section.</p>
<p>The Seller and Oreaka.vn compare and check the successful transactions (paid and no complaints or returns) in which the Buyer has purchased the Seller's Products.</p>
<p>Oreka confirms the seller's payment information. Oreka is responsible for transferring the money to the seller after deducting the commission calculated on the successfully sold product.</p>
<p>- Payment period</p>
<p>(i) Payment will be made within 5-7 working days from the date the seller sends a valid payment request.</p>
<p>(ii) Each Party will be responsible for bank fees and related tax obligations of each Party.</p>
<p>V. Transaction Security<br>The Oreka.vn website builds a transaction security mechanism as follows:</p>
<p>The Company uses member information verification including payment information and personal information. To ensure that transactions are successfully completed, and to minimize possible risks, the Company complies with the following procedures:</p>
<p>- Member protection: The ordering system is designed so that this function cannot be performed until the system ensures information security for the buyer when placing an order.</p>
<p>- As soon as the buyer clicks the "Payment" button, all information related to the order, including all personal information, and payment details, will go through all encrypted formats according to Oreka.vn standards.</p>
<p>- Members should not provide payment details to anyone via email or other means. The Company is not responsible for any loss that a member may suffer due to the exchange of information related to payment by any means.</p>
<p>- Members are not allowed to use any programs, tools, or any other form of interference in the Company's system or change the data structures. Absolutely do not distribute, disseminate, use any activities that interfere with causing damage, or violate the foundation of business transactions on the Company's website. Any violations will be handled according to the terms of this regulation and relevant legal provisions.</p>
<p>- All parties participating with the Company must keep all transaction information confidential, except in cases where the law requires the provision of information.</p>
<p>Oreka creates a safe and user-friendly marketplace. Oreka does not pay the seller until the buyer receives the goods and both the buyer and the seller submit reviews to each other. If an item is not as described, the buyer can file a complaint with Oreka within 3 days. First, discuss with the seller and give them a chance to fix the problem. If no agreement is reached after 3 business days, Oreka will intervene to resolve the issue. Buyers are only protected if they follow the Buyer Guidelines:</p>
<p>- Do not purchase prohibited items.</p>
<p>- Inspect the item upon delivery.</p>
<p>If you do not contact Oreka within 3 days of receiving the item, the order is automatically confirmed as completed.</p>
<p>About payment security</p>
<p>Buyer payment information such as payment card number, account number, date of issue, expiration date, CVV number will not be saved on the Oreka.vn system. When the buyer chooses any payment gateway, the Oreka.vn system will transfer the Buyer to that payment gateway. The Buyer's card information will be entered at the payment gateway. Therefore, this information will be secured by the payment gateway service provider according to the Company's regulations. Before paying at the payment gateway, Buyers need to read the regulations publicly announced on the payment gateway.</p>
<p>After the Buyer pays at the payment gateway, the system connected between the payment gateway and the Oreka.vn website will return to Oreka.vn a data message informing whether the Buyer has successfully or unsuccessfully paid for the order purchased at Oreka.vn. Based on that data message, Oreka.vn will confirm or not confirm the buyer's order.</p>
<p>Oreka.vn is not responsible for the security of information related to the Buyer's payment card information. Oreka.vn will assist the Buyer in providing information about the paid order to the payment gateway in case of a dispute between the two parties.</p>
<p>VI. Protection of Buyer's personal information<br>1. Purpose and scope of collection</p>
<p>During the process of providing services, We will/may collect personal data about Buyers in the following cases:</p>
<p>- When Buyers register/access and/or use our website</p>
<p>- When Buyers submit any forms, including applications or other forms related to any of our products and services, online or otherwise;</p>
<p>- When Buyers sign any agreement or provide other documents or information related to the interaction between Buyers and us, or when Buyers use our products and services;</p>
<p>- When Buyers make transactions through our Services;</p>
<p>- When Buyers provide feedback or send us complaints;</p>
<p>- When Buyers send us their personal data for any reason.</p>
<p>Personal data that Oreka.vn may collect includes:</p>
<p>- Full name;</p>
<p>- Email address;</p>
<p>- Date of birth;</p>
<p>- Billing address;</p>
<p>- Bank account and payment information;</p>
<p>- Phone number;</p>
<p>- Gender;</p>
<p>- Information sent by or related to the device(s) used to access our Services or Platform.</p>
<p>The collection of information is for the purpose of serving the Buyer's transactions and activities related to the website. Buyers will be responsible for the security and retention of all activities using the service under their registered name, password and email box. In addition, Buyers are responsible for promptly notifying Oreka.vn of any unauthorized use, abuse, security breach, or retention of third-party registration names and passwords for appropriate action.</p>
<p>2. Scope of information use</p>
<p>Oreka.vn uses the information provided by Buyers to:</p>
<p>- Provide services to Buyers;</p>
<p>- Send notifications about information exchange activities between Buyers and Oreka.vn;</p>
<p>- Prevent activities that destroy Buyer user accounts or activities that impersonate Buyers;</p>
<p>- Contact and resolve with Buyers in special cases.</p>
<p>- Do not use Buyer's personal information for purposes other than confirmation and contact related to transactions at Oreka.vn.</p>
<p>- In case of legal requirements: Oreka.vn is responsible for cooperating to provide Buyer's personal information when requested by judicial agencies including: Procuracy, court, police investigation agency related to any violation of the law by the Buyer. In addition, no one has the right to infringe on Buyer's personal information.</p>
<p>3. Information storage time</p>
<p>Buyer's personal data will be stored until there is a request for cancellation or the Buyer logs in and cancels it. In all other cases, Buyer's personal information will be kept confidential on Oreka.vn's server.</p>
<p>4. People or organizations that can access personal information</p>
<p>The subjects that can access the personal information of Buyers/Buyers are in one of the following cases:</p>
<p>- Oreka Vietnam Co., Ltd.</p>
<p>- Suppliers who have signed a contract to perform part of the services provided by Oreka Vietnam Co., Ltd., such as transportation and payment services. These units will receive information according to the contract agreement (maybe part or all of the information depending on the terms of the contract) to support users in using the services provided by the Company.</p>
<p>- State agencies when requesting the Company to provide user information to serve the investigation process.</p>
<p>- The buyer and seller have a dispute and request the Company to be the mediator.</p>
<p>5. Address of the unit collecting and managing personal information</p>
<p>Oreka Vietnam Co., Ltd.<br>Head office: B2-25 Vinhomes Gardenia, Ham Nghi Street, Cau Dien, Nam Tu Liem, Hanoi<br>Email: hotro@oreka.vn<br>6. Means and tools for users to access and edit their personal data.</p>
<p>Buyers have the right to self-check, update, adjust or cancel their personal information by logging into their account and editing personal information.</p>
<p>Buyers have the right to send complaints about the disclosure of personal information to a third party to the Board of Directors of Oreka.vn. Upon receiving these responses, Oreka.vn will reconfirm the information, be responsible for answering the reasons and instructing Buyers to restore and secure the information.</p>
<p>Email: <a href="mailto:lienhe@oreka.vn">lienhe@oreka.vn</a></p>
<p>7. Commitment to protect Buyer personal information</p>
<p>Buyer personal information on Oreka.vn is committed to absolute confidentiality according to Oreka.vn's personal information protection policy. The collection and use of each Buyer's information is only carried out with the consent of that Buyer, except in cases where the law provides otherwise.</p>
<p>Do not use, transfer, provide or disclose to any third party any personal information of the Buyer without the Buyer's consent.</p>
<p>In the event that the information storage server is hacked, leading to the loss of Buyer's personal data, Oreka.vn will be responsible for notifying the authorities to promptly investigate and handle the matter and notify the Buyer.</p>
<p>Oreka.vn Management Board requires individuals when registering/purchasing to provide full relevant personal information such as: Full name, contact address, email, ID card number, phone number, account number, payment card number, etc., and is responsible for the legality of the above information. Oreka.vn Management Board is not responsible for and will not resolve any complaints related to the rights of that Buyer if it is determined that all personal information provided by the Buyer upon initial registration is inaccurate.</p>
<p>8. Mechanism for receiving and resolving complaints related to Buyer personal information</p>
<p>Buyers have the right to complain about the disclosure of personal information to a third party to the Management Board of the Oreka.vn E-commerce Exchange, by sending to the Company's address or via email: lienhe@oreka.vn</p>
<p>The Company is responsible for implementing technical and professional measures to verify the reflected content.</p>
<p>Processing time for feedback related to Buyer personal information is 15 days.</p>
<p>VII. Bad information management<br>1. Member regulations:<br>Members will be responsible for the security and retention of all activities using the service under their registered name and password. Members are responsible for promptly notifying the Oreka.vn Website of any unauthorized use, abuse, security breach, or retention of third-party registered names and passwords for appropriate resolution.</p>
<p>Members who post articles about products and services in the wrong category will be notified by email and transferred to the appropriate category by the Oreka.vn Website Administration Board.</p>
<p>Members shall not use the services of the Oreka.vn Website for illegal, unreasonable, fraudulent, threatening, illegal information gathering, destructive purposes, creating and spreading viruses that damage the system, configuration, and information transmission of the Oreka.vn Website or use its services for speculative purposes, market manipulation, creating fake orders and offers, including for the purpose of judging market demand. In case of violation, members shall be responsible for their actions before the law.</p>
<p>Members shall not change, edit, assign, copy, disseminate, distribute, provide and create similar tools of the services provided by the Oreka.vn E-commerce Platform to a third party without the consent of the Oreka.vn Website in this Regulation.</p>
<p>Members are not allowed to act in any way that damages the reputation of the Oreka.vn E-commerce Platform, such as causing disunity among members by using a second registration name, through a third party, or propagating and disseminating information that is not beneficial to the reputation of the Oreka.vn E-commerce Platform.</p>
<p>2. Regulations on seller information</p>
<p>Sellers are responsible for updating their personal/business information and posting products using their own accounts. However, the seller account must be verified before posting products. Individuals will need to verify their ID card/CCCD/Passport, and business Sellers will need to verify their Business Registration Certificate.</p>
<p>The administration department will review the seller's information and send a notification requesting ID or Business Registration Certificate verification if the seller has not done so.</p>
<p>3. Regulations on posted products and services</p>
<p>Products posted by Sellers on Oreka.vn are not in the following categories:</p>
<p>List of prohibited products for trading:</p>
<p>- Anything illegal</p>
<p>- Drugs including, but not limited to:</p>
<p>+ Illegal drugs or narcotics<br>+ Prescription drugs or devices, pharmaceuticals or drugs dispensed by pharmacists without a doctor's prescription or other forms of compliance.<br>+ Products, tools, or services offered or intended to be used to create or consume drugs<br>+ Ingredients grown for drugs (such as marijuana seeds)</p>
<p>- Beverages, foods, homemade treats, supplements, vitamins, diet products, muscle enhancers, home remedies, and homemade cosmetics (anything edible):</p>
<p>+ Listings or descriptions of items offering exotic cures such as â€œanti-aging,â€ â€œcancer protection,â€<br>+ Listings making false health claims or misusing terminology (such as â€œvirus,â€ â€œepidemicâ€)<br>+ Items containing cannabidiol (CBD)</p>
<p>- Inflated-priced products, when the item is listed to profit from tragedy and natural disasters (such as â€œCoronavirus outbreak,â€ â€œCentral Vietnam floods,â€ etc.)</p>
<p>- Stolen goods:</p>
<p>+ Note: If a purchased item is reported stolen, the victim or another party may request its return and the item may be seized as required by law.</p>
<p>- Counterfeit or third-party intellectual property infringements:</p>
<p>+ Listings of non-branded, non-genuine, counterfeit, fake, or copied items<br>+ Copyrighted items, including crafts or other items with copyrighted characters, trademark logos, etc.<br>+ Note: For branded products, a serial number or receipt must be included when listing the item.</p>
<p>- Firearms include:</p>
<p>+ Firearms and firearm parts;<br>+ Knives such as switchblades, butterfly knives, knives concealed in other objects or made of materials that cannot be detected by metal detectors</p>
<p>+ Explosives or military orders</p>
<p>+ Self-defense weapons</p>
<p>- Alcoholic beverages</p>
<p>- Tobacco products:</p>
<p>+ Cigarettes<br>+ E-cigarettes, e-hookahs, or other vaporizers that contain nicotine or are associated with the use of tobacco or nicotine<br>+ Non-nicotine vaporizers</p>
<p>- Items used for identity theft (such as account logins, user credentials, and/or account access codes)</p>
<p>- Items that you do not own:</p>
<p>+ Dropshipping products.<br>+ Ads or listings of items that are being sought<br>+ Items you do not currently have that are being ordered<br>+ Coupons</p>
<p>- Items that pose a safety hazard:</p>
<p>+ Note: Flammable or flammable liquids and any other items requiring special shipping or handling instructions must be shipped by you.</p>
<p>- Products designed to circumvent copyright protection techniques or facilitate the unauthorized use of copyrighted material (such as â€œmod chipsâ€ that break the encryption on computer games to allow the playing of unlicensed copies of games)</p>
<p>- Age-restricted products or products that require legal approval, seller/buyer registration, or a license to be sold</p>
<p>- Gambling, including lotteries and shady trading</p>
<p>- Financial products and services such as:</p>
<p>+ Bonds, securities, warranties, and insurance<br>+ All circulating currency of any denomination except collectibles<br>+ Precious metals including bullion or bars<br>+ Buying and selling gift cards or prepaid cards</p>
<p>- Live animals or animal parts (such as ivory or shark fins)</p>
<p>- Any product that contains computer viruses, malware, or spyware</p>
<p>- Digital items - any item where the order is made electronically or requires a download, such as:</p>
<p>+ E-books, PDFs, user-generated content (UGC), or online game items</p>
<p>+ Exception: Digital game items listed through Oreka.</p>
<p>- Humans, human body parts, organs, cells, blood, body fluids and contaminated human objects such as used underwear</p>
<p>- Obscene products:</p>
<p>+ Pornographic items, such as sex toys and fetishes</p>
<p>- Violent products:</p>
<p>+ Items, listings, photos or content that promote or glorify hatred, violence, racism or discrimination (at our discretion)</p>
<p>List of conditional trading products:</p>
<p>- For martial arts sports equipment, the Seller must be a sports equipment store or sports equipment manufacturer.</p>
<p>- For sex items such as condoms, they can be sold as a pharmacy, but sex toys and aphrodisiacs cannot be sold.</p>
<p>- For copyrighted software items such as accounts, software, etc., they must be sold by a company with a clear business license. Individuals are not allowed to sell this item.</p>
<p>Oreka Ad Listings will not post:</p>
<p>- Advertisements that lack aesthetics, are contrary to the historical traditions, culture, ethics, and customs of Vietnam.</p>
<p>- Advertisements that insult the reputation, honor, and dignity of organizations and individuals.</p>
<p>- Advertisements that use images, words, and writings of individuals without the consent of those individuals, except in cases permitted by law.</p>
<p>- Advertisements that are incorrect or cause confusion about the business capacity, the ability to provide products, goods, and services of organizations and individuals trading in products, goods, and services; about the quantity, quality, price, uses, designs, packaging, trademarks, origins, types, service methods, and warranty periods of products, goods, and services that have been registered or announced.</p>
<p>- Advertising by using the method of direct comparison of price, quality, efficiency of using products, goods, services with the price, quality, efficiency of using products, goods, services of the same type of other organizations, individuals.</p>
<p>- Advertising with unfair competition content according to the provisions of the law on competition.</p>
<p>- Advertising violating the law on intellectual property.</p>
<p>4. Mechanism for reviewing and controlling information of Oreka Management Board for products posted on the platforms:</p>
<p>Seller accounts must have verified information of ID card/ CCCD/ Passport if they are individuals or business registration certificate if they are enterprises.</p>
<p>For product information, Sellers need to provide complete information as required.</p>
<p>The content censorship department will verify and authenticate the content to be posted by comparing it with the regulations on posting information, the list of prohibited and restricted products and services. Violations of the content will be rejected by the Censorship Department or removed from the Website. In some cases, the seller's product is a conditional business product, the seller will be required to provide appropriate licenses to trade that product.</p>
<p>Regarding the censorship of Buyer feedback information, when receiving feedback about the seller's product. The Company will directly contact the person who is reflecting to receive and verify the information. Oreka will conduct a reconciliation with the seller to clarify issues related to the Buyer's feedback. After clearly identifying the issues, Oreka will work with the Buyer to notify the results (depending on the level of violation, there will be actions to ensure the rights of consumers such as: product compensation, ....).</p>
<p>When detecting incorrect information content, information about the Seller's products/services that are not as described, the Content Moderation Department will proceed to delete that content and send a warning to the Seller. Depending on the case, if it is determined that the error caused by the seller causes harm to the Buyer or to the Oreka.vn Platform, the seller may be required to compensate.</p>
<p>Oreka.vn will have the right to remove the Seller's products and services if they violate the posting regulations. Services that do not comply with the prescribed categories will be deleted or Oreka.vn will move them to another category that it deems appropriate.</p>
<p>Oreka.vn reserves the right to remove additional content that violates the posting regulations of the Website. Oreka reserves the right to decide whether to keep or remove the content posted on this website and will notify the seller and Buyer.</p>
<p>5. Sanctions if the seller violates the regulations</p>
<p>If the first violation: Oreka.vn will send an email to the violating seller, along with the violated content to notify and delete the violating content.</p>
<p>If the second violation: Oreka.vn will send an email/system notification to the violating seller, along with the violated content, and close the seller's booth/account. The seller will have to contact the oreka.vn administration to resolve related issues. Oreka.vn will consider reopening the booth for the seller based on the measures taken by the seller.</p>
<p>If the third violation: Oreka.vn will lock the account and terminate the agreement with the seller. The seller is responsible for fulfilling the obligations under the agreement</p>
<p>VIII. Responsibility in case of technical errors<br>The Oreka.vn website is committed to making every effort to ensure the safety and stability of the entire technical system. However, in case of an incident due to Oreka.vn's fault, Oreka.vn will immediately take measures to ensure the rights of members.</p>
<p>When making transactions on Oreka.vn, members are required to follow the instructions correctly.</p>
<p>The Oreka.vn Website Management Board is committed to providing the best quality of service to members participating in transactions. In case of technical errors, software errors or other objective errors that prevent members from participating in transactions, members must notify the Website Management Board at the email address: lienhe@oreka.vn, we will fix the error as soon as possible, creating conditions for members to participate in transactions at Oreka.vn.</p>
<p>However, the Oreka.vn Website Management Board will not be responsible for resolving cases where members' notifications do not reach the Management Board, arising from technical errors, transmission errors, software errors or other errors not caused by the Management Board.</p>
<p>IX. Rights and obligations of the Oreka.vn Website Management Board providing e-commerce services<br>1. Rights of the Oreka.vn Website Management Board</p>
<p>Website Oreka.vn has the right to request the Seller to provide necessary information about the product; request to modify the product image and description in accordance with the policies and terms to post these products on the Website;</p>
<p>Website Oreka.vn has the right to make decisions on the products that the Seller wishes to trade on the Website. Oreka.vn has the full right to refuse any inappropriate or illegal products traded on the website;</p>
<p>Website Oreka.vn can temporarily suspend the provision of part or all of the service if the Seller delays payment or there is any dispute arising with the Buyer or with Oreka.vn;</p>
<p>Website Oreka.vn has the right to receive a % (percentage) of commission as agreed with the Seller and deduct the fees, charges, taxes incurred (if any) and other payable amounts under the Seller's responsibility under the contract agreement; At the same time, the Oreka.vn website has the right to temporarily withhold the seller's collection if the seller violates the obligations under the contract until the violation is remedied.</p>
<p>The Oreka.vn website has the right to immediately remove information about the Goods (Services) if there is reason to believe that the Goods (Services) provided by the seller are prohibited from trading, restricted from trading, poor quality, counterfeit goods, or infringe on the intellectual property rights of any third party or the seller violates one of the obligations stipulated in the cooperation agreement. The Oreka.vn website will carry out this removal without prior notice to the seller.</p>
<p>The Oreka.vn website has the right to request the Seller to provide information and request cooperation in the process of performing its work.</p>
<p>The Oreka.vn website will proceed to provide services to participating Buyers after completing the procedures and mandatory conditions set forth by the Oreka.vn website.</p>
<p>In case there is a basis to prove that the Buyer provides information to the Oreka.vn Website that is inaccurate, misleading, incomplete or violates the law or Vietnamese customs, the Oreka.vn Website has the right to refuse, suspend or terminate the Buyer's right to use the service.</p>
<p>The Oreka.vn Website may terminate the Buyer's rights and the right to use one or all of the Buyer's services and will notify the Buyer within at least one (01) month in case the Buyer violates the Regulations of the Oreka.vn Website or has behaviors that affect business activities on the Oreka.vn Website.</p>
<p>Website Oreka.vn can immediately terminate the Buyer's right to use the service and Buyer rights if Oreka.vn discovers that the Buyer has gone bankrupt, been convicted or is serving a sentence, in case the Buyer continues to operate, it may cause legal liability for Website Oreka.vn, has fraudulent activities, counterfeiting, causing market disruption, causing disunity among other Buyers of Website Oreka.vn, activities that violate current laws of Vietnam. In case of termination of Buyer rights and service use rights, all certificates and rights granted to the Buyer will automatically expire and be terminated. The Seller grants Oreka.vn the right to use the name, logo, and related information on marketing materials and as a reference for the work/joint venture that Oreka.vn provides, and the right to publish and publicize all progress and cooperation work in the Contract, provided that trade secrets and business information are not disclosed without the Seller's consent.</p>
<p>The Oreka.vn website holds the copyright to use the services and content on the Oreka.vn website in accordance with the legal regulations on intellectual property protection in Vietnam. All logos and content in different languages â€‹â€‹are owned by the Oreka.vn website. Any act of copying, using and illegally disseminating the above ownership rights is strictly prohibited.</p>
<p>Website Oreka.vn reserves the right to change the service price list and payment method during the service provision period for Buyers according to the needs and capabilities of Website Oreka.vn and will notify Buyers one (01) month in advance.</p>
<p>The right to be paid in full and on time as stipulated in the contract. The right to request remediation and compensation in case the Seller violates any obligations under the Contract and/or causes damage to Oreka.vn.</p>
<p>Oreka.vn has the right to carry out all marketing activities such as leaflets, posters, banners and trade promotion campaigns, at the Seller's business location; as well as use the Seller's name in marketing activities.</p>
<p>Oreka.vn has the right to request the Seller and Buyers not to disclose or provide information that is detrimental to the interests of Oreka.vn.</p>
<p>2. Obligations and responsibilities of the Oreka.vn Website Management Board<br>The Oreka.vn Website is responsible for providing services to the Seller after completing the procedures and mandatory conditions for the Seller's information and the products the Seller intends to post on the Oreka.vn Website.</p>
<p>Website Oreka.vn must ensure that the website is operated legally and that the relevant Certificates and Licenses are issued in accordance with the provisions of law;</p>
<p>Website Oreka.vn is obliged to provide technical support and answer Sellers' questions quickly and professionally with expertise, professional skills and knowledge within the scope related to transactions on the website; support Sellers with website features when requested. Website Oreka.vn must arrange staff and contact points to support and guide users on how to manage operations as well as resolve problems during the user's participation on the Website.</p>
<p>Pay the collected amount to the seller according to the cooperation agreement.</p>
<p>Do not disclose or provide information that harms the interests of the seller.</p>
<p>Website Oreka.vn is responsible for building and implementing a "mechanism for checking and monitoring to ensure that the information provided by the Seller on the e-commerce website is carried out accurately and completely" according to the provisions of Clause 4, Article 36 of Decree 52/2013/ND-CP. Ensure that the Website will be operated, operated and maintained in accordance with Vietnam's national quality standards smoothly and meet the service provided under the terms of the Contract</p>
<p>Website Oreka.vn is responsible for building a number of main tasks such as: research, design, purchase of hardware and software equipment, Internet connection, building policies to serve the operation of Website Oreka.vn under the permitted conditions and scope. Website Oreka.vn will implement and cooperate with Sellers in building a system of services and utility tools to serve the transactions of participating Buyers and users on Website Oreka.vn</p>
<p>Website Oreka.vn is responsible for acting as an intermediary in mediation if there is a dispute between Seller and Buyer. Website will receive feedback and complaints from Buyers and check the content. If the feedback is found to be correct, Website will request Sellers to explain. Depending on the level of violation, Website Oreka.vn will have a solution to request Sellers to compensate Buyers.</p>
<p>Remove from the Oreka.vn Website information on services that violate intellectual property rights and other services that violate the law when detecting or receiving valid feedback about this information.</p>
<p>Prevent and remove from the Oreka.vn Website information on sales and services that are in the list of services and services prohibited from business according to the provisions of the Law and services with restricted business or services and services with conditions on Oreka.vn;</p>
<p>The Oreka.vn Website will try its best within the scope and conditions possible to maintain the normal operation of the Oreka.vn Website and remedy according to the terms and conditions of the Contract. However, if the above incidents occur beyond control, are force majeure events such as natural disasters, epidemics that cause damage to the Buyer, Oreka.vn shall not be held jointly responsible.</p>
<p>Oreka.vn Website will provide VAT invoices for the fully paid commission to the Seller along with Oreka.vn's monthly management report if requested by the Seller. VAT invoices must be provided within 5 working days from the date of meeting all the above conditions.</p>
<p>Coordinate with the Seller to resolve disputes between the Buyer and the Seller regarding complaints during the provision of products and services via the Oreka.vn Website. Refund service fees and ensure the rights of the Buyer by refunding fees/returning services accordingly if the fault is determined to be the Seller's. Oreka.vn will require the Seller to be obligated to compensate for the Buyer's damages when the fault is determined to be the Seller's. Oreka.vn commits that official support channels will be applied within 72 hours of receiving the support request.</p>
<p>Oreka.vn will not share the Buyer's personal data with the Seller more than the necessary information such as full name, avatar, phone number and other statistics. In case of any problem with the Buyer, the parties understand that Oreka.vn is not responsible for verifying the Buyer. However, Oreka.vn will make every effort to cooperate with the Seller and competent authorities in case Vietnamese law has regulations.</p>
<p>X. Rights and responsibilities of Sellers participating in the Oreka.vn E-commerce Service Website<br>1. Rights of Sellers participating in the Oreka.vn Website<br>After confirming the agreement on posting information on the Oreka.vn Website system, the Seller will be approved for an account to post information about their products/services on the Oreka.vn Website.</p>
<p>Sellers will be supported with training in the necessary skills to manage accounts on the Oreka.vn Website via the support hotline or email to the Oreka.vn care and consulting department if requested.</p>
<p>Have the right to use the features and utilities associated with the seller account on the Oreka.vn Website as well as the services provided by Oreka.vn.</p>
<p>Sellers can access from the Seller account at any time to monitor activities; and use the features and utilities on the Website to provide and introduce products;</p>
<p>Has the right to receive back from Oreka the amounts that Oreka has collected on behalf of the two parties according to the provisions of the Cooperation Contract between the two parties.</p>
<p>The Seller is entitled to preferential policies set forth by the Website management board or provided by third-party Sellers on the Oreka.vn Website during its operation.</p>
<p>2. Responsibilities of Sellers participating in the Oreka.vn Website<br>The Seller must provide complete information such as company name, ID card/tax code number, business line, Website (if any), ... to the Oreka.vn management board;</p>
<p>The Seller is responsible for providing the Oreka.vn Website with a copy of the business registration certificate or ID card if the Seller is an individual. In case the Seller is the owner of a brand or an authorized agent of an investor, the Seller is responsible for providing one (01) photocopy of the agency contract or distribution authorization of that investor;</p>
<p>The Seller must commit that the information and documents provided are accurate and must be originals or notarized copies of local authorities;</p>
<p>The Seller is responsible for accurately listing information about service images, prices, support policies (if any)... in a specific and clear manner;</p>
<p>Provide complete and accurate information for information posted on the Website and be responsible for any consequences caused by providing false information;</p>
<p>The products that the Seller sells on the Website must meet the business conditions, quality and other conditions according to applicable laws;</p>
<p>Any abuse by the Seller (such as intentionally not adding orders to the system, increasing or decreasing service fees without notifying the Oreka.vn Website and the Buyer, intentionally not using the Oreka.vn Website or the Seller giving a separate discount to the Buyer so that the Buyer places an order without going through the Website...) will result in the termination of the contract and the application of a contractual penalty (plus in cases where there is a basis for the Seller to give a separate discount to the Buyer to place an order on the Website).</p>
<p>Any order that is not added to the system by the Seller, leading to a conflict in the ordering of the Buyer using the Oreka.vn Website, the Seller will have to give priority to the user of the Oreka.vn Website;</p>
<p>The Seller must ensure the quantity and quality of the services committed on the Website, must adjust and improve according to the Buyer's feedback through the Website, and take full responsibility related to the goods provided;</p>
<p>The Seller is responsible for resolving complaints or disputes with the Buyer; receiving and resolving requests, complaints and lawsuits related to products on the Website, in case there are requests, complaints, lawsuits recorded on the Website or in case the Oreka.vn Administration Board sends requests, complaints, lawsuits about the Seller's products;</p>
<p>Commit to resolving all complaints of the Buyer related to the Seller's Products in a spirit of goodwill, cooperation and friendliness;</p>
<p>Exempt the Oreka.vn Website from all complaints and lawsuits related to the Seller's products;</p>
<p>The Seller may not transfer or assign its obligations hereunder without the written consent of the Oreka.vn Website;</p>
<p>Exempt and compensate Website Oreka.vn and/or its affiliates for any damages arising from the quality of products or services and/or violations by the Seller due to non-compliance with legal regulations and affecting the business operations of Website Oreka.vn, the penalty decision of the competent authority;</p>
<p>The Seller commits to comply with all local regulations related to the provision of services being traded;</p>
<p>The Seller must comply with the working hours of Website Oreka.vn, in case of changes in working schedule due to holidays or special events, the Seller must ensure to notify on Website Oreka.vn 48 hours before making the schedule change;</p>
<p>Payment between the Seller and Website Oreka.vn for each order: payment for services is made by bank transfer or according to the terms agreed by the parties. The Buyer will make payment to the Oreka.vn Website using the existing form of the Website and the Oreka.vn Administration Board will update it to the system and then make payment to the Seller after deducting the corresponding commission for the Oreka.vn Website; and</p>
<p>Coordinate with the Oreka.vn Website to resolve disputes between the Buyer and the Seller regarding complaints during the transaction process taking place via the Oreka.vn Website. The Seller is obliged to compensate the Buyer for damages when the fault is determined to be the Seller's.</p>
<p>The Seller must comply with the provisions of the law on payment, advertising, promotion, protection of intellectual property rights, protection of consumer rights and other relevant legal provisions when selling goods or providing services on Oreka.vn</p>
<p>The Seller is responsible for fully performing tax obligations according to the provisions of the law.</p>
<p>XI. Rights and responsibilities of Buyers participating in the Oreka.vn e-commerce service website</p>
<p>1. Rights of Buyers on the Oreka.vn website</p>
<p>Buyers have the right to register to create an account and have their account approved by the administrator on Oreka.vn. The account includes a unique username and password to log in to Oreka.vn and use in managing Buyer transactions at Oreka.vn such as online ordering and online payment on Oreka.vn.</p>
<p>Buyers will be guided by Oreka.vn staff to use tools and features for ordering and using other convenient services on Oreka.vn.</p>
<p>Buyers have the right to contribute opinions to Oreka.vn during the operation process. Recommendations are sent directly by letter, fax or email to Oreka.vn. Maintain timely and smooth communication with Oreka.vn for service operation.</p>
<p>Receive VAT invoice issued by Oreka.vn Seller when fully paying for goods ordered through Oreka.vn.</p>
<p>2. Obligations of Buyers Website providing Oreka.vn e-commerce services</p>
<p>Buyers will be responsible for the security and storage and all activities using the service under their registered name, password and email box.</p>
<p>Buyers are responsible for promptly notifying Oreka.vn of any unauthorized use, abuse, security breach, and storage of their registered name and password so that both parties can cooperate to handle it. In case the communication or cooperation with the Seller is not properly responded to, Oreka.vn is not responsible for any complaints about damages that occur.</p>
<p>Buyers commit that the information provided to Oreka.vn and the information posted on Oreka.vn is accurate.</p>
<p>The Buyer commits and agrees not to use Oreka.vn's services for illegal, unreasonable, fraudulent, threatening, illegal information gathering, destructive purposes, creating and spreading viruses that damage the system, configuration, and information transmission of Oreka.vn or using its services for speculative purposes, manipulating the market, creating fake orders and offers, including for the purpose of judging market demand. In case of violation, the Buyer must be responsible for his/her actions before the law.</p>
<p>The Buyer commits not to change, edit, copy, disseminate, distribute, provide and create similar tools of the services provided by Oreka.vn to a third party without the consent of Oreka.vn in this Regulation.</p>
<p>Buyers are not allowed to act in any way that damages the reputation of Oreka.vn, such as causing disunity among Buyers by using a second registration name, through a third party, or propagating and disseminating information that is not beneficial to the reputation of Oreka.vn.</p>
<p>Strictly comply with and commit to payment obligations and other obligations under the contract.</p>
<p>Comply with the terms and regulations of the Website. Buyers commit not to use other systems/solutions/websites/Websites/software that may directly conflict with Oreka.vn's interests.</p>
<p>Applicable Terms<br>Oreka.vn Website has the right and can change this Regulation by notifying the Seller and the purchasing Buyer. The member's continued use of the service after the revised Regulation is announced and implemented means that the member has accepted this revised Regulation.</p>
<p>The operating regulations will be continuously updated and supplemented by Oreka.vn and notified 5 working days before implementation/taking effect. Sellers and Buyers who are members of the Oreka.vn Website are responsible for complying with the current regulations when transacting on the Website.</p>
<p>XII. Commitment terms</p>
<p>All buyers and Sellers when using the Oreka.vn Website for online buying and selling transactions mean that the related parties have agreed to comply with this regulation.</p>
<p>For any questions, please contact the Oreka.vn Website with the information below for answers</p>
<p>Buyer support</p>
<p>Oreka.vn e-commerce trading floor<br>Oreka Vietnam Co., Ltd.<br>Head office: B2-25 Vinhomes Gardenia, Ham Nghi Street, Cau Dien, Nam Tu Liem, Hanoi<br>Email: hotro@oreka.vn<br>Phone: 0904433126</p>

#### Oreka Application on Mobile

**ID:** 20501804780313 | **Votes:** 0 | **Updated:** 31/8/2024
**URL:** [https://oreka.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/20501804780313-Oreka-Application-on-Mobile](https://oreka.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/20501804780313-Oreka-Application-on-Mobile)

<p>The Oreka App is available on all mobile platforms. You can search for "Oreka" on the app store of the platform you are using and install it.</p>
<p>Why should Sellers use the Oreka app?</p>
<p>- App-specific promotions: There are many programs for Sellers from Oreka that are only available on the app, use the app to update as soon as there is a new announcement</p>
<p>Easier to post: The posting process is minimized when posting by phone because Sellers can easily take photos of products and post them immediately.</p>
<p>Continuous information: Sellers can track the status of the shop and will know immediately when there is a new order.</p>
<p>Why should Buyers use the Oreka app?</p>
<p>More convenient: Now you just need to touch the Oreka icon to freely browse used items. The Oreka app is designed specifically for the phone experience, so it is more suitable for swiping and touching than using the website on the browser.<br>- App-exclusive promotions: New notifications about promotions on Oreka are updated continuously every hour of the day.</p>
<p>Install the Oreka app on your phone to upgrade your second-hand shopping experience!</p>

#### Privacy Policy

**ID:** 900006898683 | **Votes:** 0 | **Updated:** 31/8/2024
**URL:** [https://oreka.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/900006898683-Privacy-Policy](https://oreka.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/900006898683-Privacy-Policy)

<p>Personal Information Protection Policy</p>
<p>Purpose and Scope of Collection<br>In the process of providing services, We will/may collect personal data about Customers in the following cases:</p>
<p>- When Customers register/access and/or use Oreka's website.</p>
<p>- When Customers sign any agreement or provide other documents or information related to the interaction between Customers and Oreka, or when Customers use Oreka's products and services.</p>
<p>- When Customers make transactions through Oreka's Services.</p>
<p>- When Customers provide feedback or submit complaints to Oreka.</p>
<p>- When Customers submit their personal data to Oreka for any reason.</p>
<p>Personal data that Oreka may collect includes:</p>
<p>- Full name</p>
<p>- Email address</p>
<p>- Date of birth</p>
<p>- Address</p>
<p>- Bank account and payment information</p>
<p>- Phone number</p>
<p>- Gender</p>
<p>- Information sent by or related to the device(s) used to access the Oreka Services or Platform.</p>
<p>The collection of information is for the purpose of serving the Customer's transactions and activities related to the Oreka platform. The Customer will be responsible for the security and storage of all activities using the service under his/her registered name, password and email box. In addition, the Customer is responsible for promptly notifying Oreka of any unauthorized use, abuse, security breach, storage of third-party registered names and passwords for appropriate action.</p>
<p>Scope of information use<br>Oreka uses the information provided by the Customer to:</p>
<p>- Provide services to the Customer.</p>
<p>- Send notifications about information exchange activities between the Customer and Oreka.</p>
<p>- Prevent activities that destroy the Customer's user account or activities that impersonate the Customer.</p>
<p>- Contact and resolve with the Customer in special cases.</p>
<p>- Do not use the Customer's personal information for purposes other than confirmation and contact related to transactions at Oreka.</p>
<p>- In case of legal requirements: Oreka is responsible for cooperating to provide the Customer's personal information when requested by judicial agencies including: the Procuracy, the court, the police investigation agency related to any violation of the law by the Customer. In addition, no one has the right to infringe on the Customer's personal information.</p>
<p>Information storage time<br>Customer's personal data will be stored until there is a request for cancellation or the Customer logs in and cancels it. In all other cases, Customer's personal information will be kept confidential on Oreka's server.</p>
<p>People or organizations that can access personal information<br>The subjects that can access the personal information of Customers/Customers are in one of the following cases:</p>
<p>- Oreka Vietnam Co., Ltd.</p>
<p>- Suppliers who have signed a contract to perform part of the services provided by Oreka Vietnam Co., Ltd., such as transportation and payment services. These units will receive information according to the contract agreement (maybe part or all of the information depending on the terms of the contract) to support users in using the services provided by the Company.</p>
<p>- State agencies when requesting the Company to provide user information to serve the investigation process.</p>
<p>- The buyer and seller have a dispute and request the Company to act as the mediator.</p>
<p>Address of the unit collecting and managing personal information<br>Â· Oreka Vietnam Co., Ltd.</p>
<p>Â· Head office: B2-25 Vinhomes Gardenia, Ham Nghi Street, Cau Dien, Nam Tu Liem, Hanoi</p>
<p>Â· Email: hotro@oreka.vn</p>
<p>Means and tools for users to access and edit their personal data.</p>
<p>Customers have the right to self-check, update, adjust or cancel their personal information by logging into their account and editing personal information.</p>
<p>Customers have the right to send complaints about the disclosure of personal information to third parties to Oreka's Board of Directors. Upon receiving these responses, Oreka will reconfirm the information, be responsible for answering the reasons and instructing Customers to restore and secure the information.</p>
<p>Email: hotro@oreka.vn</p>
<p>Commitment to protecting customer personal information<br>Customer personal information on Oreka is committed to absolute confidentiality according to Oreka's personal information protection policy. The collection and use of each Customer's information is only done with the consent of that Customer, except in cases where the law provides otherwise.</p>
<p>Do not use, transfer, provide or disclose to any third party any personal information of the Customer without the Customer's consent.</p>
<p>In the event that the information storage server is hacked, leading to the loss of Customer's personal data, Oreka will be responsible for notifying the authorities to promptly investigate and handle the matter and notify the Customer.</p>
<p>Oreka's administration requires individuals to provide full relevant personal information when registering/purchasing such as: Full name, contact address, email, ID card number, phone number, account number, payment card number, etc., and is responsible for the legality of the above information. Oreka's administration is not responsible for and will not resolve any complaints related to the rights of that Customer if it is determined that all personal information provided by the Customer upon initial registration is inaccurate.</p>

<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-weight: normal;">By using our Services, you agree to abide by the rules and conduct, agreeing not to engage in the following Prohibited Conduct:</span></p>

#### Prohibited Items

**ID:** 900006898923 | **Votes:** 0 | **Updated:** 31/8/2024
**URL:** [https://oreka.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/900006898923-Prohibited-Items](https://oreka.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/900006898923-Prohibited-Items)

<p>Oreka prohibits the listing or sale of any item listed in the prohibited items list. If a Seller lists a prohibited item, it will be considered a violation of our Terms of Service regardless of whether the Seller intended it to be so. If Oreka determines that a listing is in violation or inappropriate, Oreka may, in its sole discretion, remove the listing and cancel any related transaction including termination or suspension.</p>
<p>You may not use Oreka in connection with any product, service, transaction or activity that:</p>
<ul>
<li>Violate any law or government regulation; promote or facilitate such conduct by third parties.</li>
<li>Fraudulent, deceptive, improper or predatory.</li>
<li>Threaten or damage the reputation of Oreka.</li>
<li>Violate the terms of any bank, card or electronic funds transfer network.</li>
<li>Result in or create a significant risk of chargebacks, fines, damages or other harm or liability.</li>
</ul>
<p>The list of prohibited items may be updated at Oreka's discretion. Examples of items in certain categories may also be expanded to provide better communication and experience to our users.</p>
<p>Oreka may not be used to sell any of the following products or services:</p>
<ul>
<li>Anything Illegal</li>
<li>Drugs include, but are not limited to:
<ul>
<li>Illegal drugs or substances.</li>
<li>A prescription drug or device, pharmaceutical product or drug dispensed by a pharmacist without a physician's prescription or other form of compliance.</li>
<li>Products, tools or services offered or intended to be used in the making or consumption of drugs.</li>
<li>Ingredients grown for drugs (such as cannabis seeds).</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Beverages, food, homemade foods, supplements, vitamins, diet products, muscle enhancers, home remedies and homemade cosmetics (anything edible):
<ul>
<li>Listings or descriptions of items offering exotic cures such as â€œanti-agingâ€ or â€œcancer protectionâ€.</li>
<li>Listings making false health claims or misusing terminology (such as â€œvirusâ€, â€œdiseaseâ€).</li>
<li>Items containing cannabidiol (CBD).</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Inflationary products, where the item is listed to profit from tragedy and natural disasters (e.g. â€œCoronavirus outbreakâ€, â€œCentral Vietnam floodsâ€, etc.)</li>
<li>Stolen goods:
<ul>
<li>Note: If a purchased item is reported stolen, the victim or another party may request its return and the item may be subject to forfeiture as required by law.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Counterfeit goods or goods that infringe third party intellectual property rights:
<ul>
<li>Listings of non-branded, non-genuine, counterfeit, fake, or copied items</li>
<li>Items that infringe copyright, including handmade items or other items with copyright symbols, trademark logos, etc.</li>
<li>Note: For branded products, a serial number or receipt is required when listing the item.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Weapons include:
<ul>
<li>Firearms and parts of firearms.</li>
<li>Knives such as switchblades, butterfly knives, knives concealed in other objects or made of materials that cannot be detected by metal detectors.</li>
<li>Explosives or military orders.</li>
<li>Self-defense weapons.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Alcoholic Beverages</li>
<li>Tobacco Products:
<ul>
<li>Cigarettes.</li>
<li>E-cigarettes, e-hookahs or other vapor devices that contain nicotine or are associated with the use of tobacco or nicotine.</li>
<li>Nicotine-free vaporizers.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Items used for identity theft (such as account logins, user credentials, and/or account access tokens).</li>
<li>Items not owned by you:
<ul>
<li>Dropshipping products.</li>
<li>Ads or listings of items being searched for.</li>
<li>Items you don't currently have that are being ordered.</li>
<li>Coupons.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Items that pose a safety hazard:
<ul>
<li>Note: Flammable or flammable liquids and any other items requiring special shipping or handling instructions must be shipped by yourself.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Products designed to circumvent copyright protection techniques or facilitate the unauthorized use of copyrighted material (such as â€œmod chipsâ€ that break the encryption on computer games to allow the playing of unlicensed copies of games).</li>
<li>Age-restricted products or products that require legal approval, seller/buyer registration, or a license to be sold.</li>
<li>Gambling, including lotteries and shady trading</li>
<li>Financial products and services such as:
<ul>
<li>Bonds, securities, warrants and insurance.</li>
<li>All circulating currency of any denomination except collectibles.</li>
<li>Precious metals including bullion or ingots.</li>
<li>Buy and sell gift cards or prepaid cards.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Live animals or animal parts (such as ivory or shark fins).</li>
<li>Any product that contains computer viruses, malware or spyware.</li>
<li>Digital items - any item where the order is made electronically or requires a download, such as:
<ul>
<li>Ebooks, PDFs, user-generated content (UGC), or online game items.</li>
<li>Exception: Digital game items listed through Oreka.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Humans, human body parts, organs, cells, blood, body fluids and contaminated human objects such as used underwear.</li>
<li>Obscene products:
<ul>
<li>Erotic items, such as sex toys and fetishes.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Violent products:
<ul>
<li>Items, listings, photos or content that promote or glorify hatred, violence, racism or discrimination (as determined by us).</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<p>Note: Any item may be removed at the company's discretion.</p>

#### Safety Guidelines

**ID:** 900006899483 | **Votes:** 0 | **Updated:** 31/8/2024
**URL:** [https://oreka.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/900006899483-Safety-Guidelines](https://oreka.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/900006899483-Safety-Guidelines)

<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-weight: normal;">We strive to provide a safe, secure and enjoyable marketplace for buyers and sellers. If a transaction goes wrong, someone is trying to scam someone else, or if you notice any Prohibited Products or Prohibited Behavior, send us a message at hotro@oreka.vn and we will be happy to help.</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-weight: normal;">Â </span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><strong>Online Safety:</strong></p>
<ul>
<li class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-weight: normal;">Do not share your personal contact information, such as phone numbers or email addresses, with anyone. We cannot assist with interactions outside the Oreka App or website</span></li>
<li class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-weight: normal;">Contact your buyer or seller via our App/web messaging feature, to ensure there is a record of the communication.</span></li>
<li class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-weight: normal;">Use a credit card instead of a debit card to make online purchases. Credit cards often have better security features and purchase protections, and your credit provider is more likely to provide refunds for fraudulent transactions.</span></li>
<li class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-weight: normal;">Come up with a strong password and change it regularly. Passwords that are non-dictionary phrases and include numbers and special characters are the strongest. Do not use the same password for multiple accounts or repeat passwords.</span></li>
<li class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-weight: normal;">Never share your Oreka account or password with anyone, including third-party websites. We will never ask you for your password.</span></li>
<li class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-weight: normal;">Do not click on links sent via email and log in to your Oreka account by clicking on a link. The safest way to log in to your Oreka account is to go directly to Oreka.vn and log in there.</span></li>
<li class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-weight: normal;">Go directly to our official website or app.</span></li>
<li class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-weight: normal;">If you allow your children to use your account, closely supervise their purchases and interactions on Oreka.</span></li>
<li class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-weight: normal;">Before buying online, read the listing and look at the photo(s) carefully. Read the reviews left about the seller. Ask the seller any questions before you pay.</span></li>
<li class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-weight: normal;">Report any problematic or prohibited items.</span></li>
</ul>
<p class="MsoNormal"><strong>Financial Safety:</strong></p>
<ul>
<li class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-weight: normal;">Never provide your personal financial (payment) information or contact information to another user, especially if they are requesting it outside of our website.</span></li>
<li><span style="font-weight: normal;">To protect you from becoming a victim of fraud, transactions must be made through Orekaâ€™s platforms. We do not support or protect transactions where the payment is transmitted outside of our website.</span></li>
<li class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-weight: normal;">Avoid transferring money to people you do not know, in situations that seem â€œtoo good to be true,â€ or to help resolve an â€œemergencyâ€ involving a friend or family member. This may involve a request to review an item you have not yet received.</span></li>
<li class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-weight: normal;">Regularly review your financial statements for suspicious activity. Contact Oreka immediately if you see any unauthorized charges.</span></li>
<li class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-weight: normal;">Check the item thoroughly upon delivery. Buyers have 3 days from the date of delivery to request a return. After 3 days have passed or the buyer has rated the transaction, all sales are final.</span></li>
<li class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-weight: normal;">Check your item before rating the seller, especially for expensive items or electronics.</span></li>
<li class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-weight: normal;">Some phone service providers may check to see if a phone has been reported stolen.</span></li>
<li class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-weight: normal;">Expensive brands often have brand information online to verify authenticity.</span></li>
</ul>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-weight: normal;">If you suspect you may have been a victim of fraud or other criminal activity, please call us at (+84) 90-4433 126 or report your suspicions to law enforcement.</span></p>
