#### Shipping policy

**ID:** 37108971773593 | **Votes:** 0 | **Updated:** 31/8/2024
**URL:** [https://oreka.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/37108971773593-Shipping-policy](https://oreka.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/37108971773593-Shipping-policy)

<p><strong>1. Delivery coverage</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>Domestic: Oreka is committed to providing nationwide shipping services, including urban and rural areas. All orders will be processed and delivered on time.</li>
<li>International: Currently, we do not support international shipping. However, we are constantly expanding and will provide this service soon.</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>2. Processing and delivery time</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>Order processing: After the order is confirmed, the shipping unit will pick up the goods within 1-2 business days. Holidays or weekends may affect the processing time.</li>
<li>Delivery: Delivery time ranges from 3-7 business days depending on the location. In remote or inaccessible areas, delivery time may be longer than expected.</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>3. Shipping fee</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>Calculation: Shipping fee will be automatically calculated based on product weight, size and delivery location. The fee will be clearly displayed before the buyer confirms the purchase.</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>4. Tracking orders</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>Tracking information: After your order is shipped, you can track the status of your order through our system.</li>
<li>Contact support: If you encounter any problems during the delivery process, you can immediately contact our customer support team via email or hotline.</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>5. Return and exchange policy</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>Return conditions: If the product you receive is not as described, damaged or has quality problems, you have the right to request a return within 3 days from the date of receipt.</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>6. Quality commitment</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>Oreka commits that all products are carefully packaged and quality checked before being delivered to customers. We always listen and receive all feedback to continuously improve the quality of service.</li>
</ul>

A product sales contract is formed with Seller when Buyer completes the steps to purchase the product as described in the Service, but before Buyer makes payment. Seller and Buyer may not assign the contract to a third party, use it as a security, or otherwise transfer their rights and obligations arising under the contract.</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-weight: normal;">Â </span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-weight: normal;">Oreka's role. Seller agrees that Oreka and Oreka's payment processing system act as Seller's agent in processing payments for transactions. Buyer's obligations to Buyer shall be deemed to have ended upon Oreka's receipt of the purchase payment (except Buyer's obligations in the event of a chargeback or other reversal of payment) and a review.</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-weight: normal;">Â </span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-weight: normal;">Review. Once a product has been received by Buyer, Buyer shall promptly review Seller. Once Buyer has reviewed Seller, Seller shall promptly review Buyer. Reviews must be provided by Buyer and Seller in order for Seller to receive its payment. If the Buyer does not rate the Seller within the specified time frame, Oreka will automatically rate the Seller to avoid delays in completing the payment.</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-weight: normal;">Â </span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-weight: normal;">Payment to Seller. Once both the Buyer and Seller's ratings are complete, Oreka and the payment processing system will process the payment to the Seller. Oreka will commercially attempt to credit the Seller's earnings balance to Oreka within ten (10) business days of Oreka receiving notification that the payment has cleared. Oreka will initiate the transfer of earnings from the balance to the Seller's bank account upon the Seller's request. Oreka may request the Seller's User Information to ensure the safety of the transfer and purchase, and may withhold earnings until the Seller's User Information is verified and confirmed. Oreka may also withhold funds if it receives a fraud or chargeback notification.</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-weight: normal;">11. General Charges</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-weight: normal;">All information regarding final transaction and/or shipping charges is communicated to the User at the time of transaction. Charges are communicated to the Seller at the time of posting, but may vary depending on shipping taxes, changes in other charges, or changes made by the Seller. Charges will be deducted from the Seller's earnings upon completion of the transaction, and will be communicated on the sales receipt. The Buyer is informed of the total amount of the order, including charges and taxes, in the order summary prior to payment. Charges will be included in the total payment amount. It is the User's responsibility to review the charges before accepting the final Sales Contract.</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-weight: normal;">Â </span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-weight: normal;">In general, charges are as follows:</span></p>

#### Can I change a rating I left?

**ID:** 900006621183 | **Votes:** 0 | **Updated:** 15/8/2024
**URL:** [https://oreka.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/900006621183-Can-I-change-a-rating-I-left](https://oreka.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/900006621183-Can-I-change-a-rating-I-left)

<p>Once a review is submitted, the transaction is complete. From that point on, you cannot change or delete your review. Your review will be deleted if it violates the following: inappropriate language, offensive language, insults, harassment of individuals or groups, etc.</p>

#### How do I rate?

**ID:** 900005677966 | **Votes:** 0 | **Updated:** 15/8/2024
**URL:** [https://oreka.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/900005677966-How-do-I-rate](https://oreka.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/900005677966-How-do-I-rate)

<p>After the order has been successfully delivered, you can rate the transaction by clicking "Rate".</p>
<p>If Oreka does not receive a rating from you after 3 days, the order will be automatically rated.</p>
<p>The order will be completed after the rating is done.</p>
<p>In case you want a refund or complaint, please do not rate, click the "Complaint" button or contact Oreka immediately via hotro@oreka.vn or hotline/zalo 0904433126.</p>

## ğŸ“‚ Seller Flow

### ğŸ“‹ Listing

#### About item conditions

**ID:** 900005677146 | **Votes:** 0 | **Updated:** 15/8/2024
**URL:** [https://oreka.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/900005677146-About-item-conditions](https://oreka.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/900005677146-About-item-conditions)

<p>Please describe the condition of the product accurately according to the following definitions:</p>
<p>* New: New with tags, unopened box/package, unused.<br>* Like new: New with tags, unopened box/package, unused.<br>* Good: Used, fully functional, working well (may have some minor scratches)<br>* Average: Used, fully functional. Many flaws or minor defects.<br>* Poor: Used. Many flaws. May be damaged (mention details if damaged).</p>
<p>If the product has defects, breaks, tears, etc., please detail these in the "Product Description" section (should be accompanied by corresponding images/videos). The more detailed information you provide to Buyers, the less likely they are to complain or give a low rating after they receive the item.</p>
<p>In addition, honest product descriptions will also help Oreka protect Sellers more easily. If the product received by the Buyer matches the product description posted by the Seller, Oreka commits to fully pay the Seller for the transaction.</p>

#### How to set price

**ID:** 900005677386 | **Votes:** 0 | **Updated:** 5/8/2024
**URL:** [https://oreka.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/900005677386-How-to-set-price](https://oreka.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/900005677386-How-to-set-price)

<p>1. All prices on Oreka are listed in Vietnamese Dong.</p>
<p>2. The lowest price is set at 20,000 VND for an item.</p>
<p>3. Do not set fake prices. The posted product price must reflect the real value of that product. Any act of setting fake prices or fake prices for the purpose of unfair competition will be banned.</p>
<p>4. In the case of an item with many variants, the price of that item should correspond to the size, color, weight, etc.</p>
<p>Please carefully research the market price first if you are still hesitant in deciding on the item price.</p>
<p>Many Buyers also research prices and compare to your product before they place an order, so let's set the most attractive prices.</p>
<p>Â </p>
<p>Â </p>
<p>Â </p>
<p>Â </p>

#### Listing Gets Removed

#### Photo & video uploading rules

**ID:** 900006620523 | **Votes:** 0 | **Updated:** 5/8/2024
**URL:** [https://oreka.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/900006620523-Photo-video-uploading-rules](https://oreka.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/900006620523-Photo-video-uploading-rules)

<p>Requirements for product photos/videos:</p>
<p>- The product should be photographed/videoed by the Seller directly. Avoid using photos taken from the product's official website or from other Sellers.</p>
<p>- If the product has a defect, take a close-up, clear photo to avoid future complaints.</p>
<p>- If there are multiple items posted at the same time, take a photo or video of each item.</p>
<p>- DO NOT post your address, phone number, email or any personal information in the product description or on the product photos/videos.</p>
<p>- If the item delivered to the Buyer is not the same as the photo/video posted by the Seller, the Buyer has the right to return the item and the Seller is responsible for the two-way shipping costs.</p>
<p>Â </p>

#### Product display period

**ID:** 900006620243 | **Votes:** 0 | **Updated:** 15/8/2024
**URL:** [https://oreka.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/900006620243-Product-display-period](https://oreka.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/900006620243-Product-display-period)

<p>Each product listed on Oreka will automatically expire after 60 days (from the last edit).</p>
<p>To keep the product on Oreka, simply refresh the product and we will extend the visibility for that product for another 60 days.</p>

#### Shipping fee

**ID:** 900006620263 | **Votes:** 0 | **Updated:** 15/8/2024
**URL:** [https://oreka.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/900006620263-Shipping-fee](https://oreka.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/900006620263-Shipping-fee)

<p>Seller can choose Seller pays shipping or Buyer pays shipping.</p>
<p>If the product is free shipping, Seller will pay shipping for the order.</p>
<p>If the product is not free shipping, Buyer will have to pay additional shipping costs when receiving the order.</p>
<p>In case the product is returned to Seller because the product received by Buyer does not match the posted product description, Seller will have to pay the shipping costs for the outbound and return trips.</p>
<p>By default, Oreka will be responsible for shipping the product, however, for bulky products, please contact Oreka for instructions on self-shipping.</p>

### ğŸ“‹ Seller Guidelines

#### Cancellation Policy for Sellers

**ID:** 50775242218137 | **Votes:** 0 | **Updated:** 18/9/2025
**URL:** [https://oreka.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/50775242218137-Cancellation-Policy-for-Sellers](https://oreka.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/50775242218137-Cancellation-Policy-for-Sellers)

<p>To enhance service quality and ensure a reliable shopping experience, Oreka will apply the Order Cancellation Rate Policy for sellers starting from <strong>October 1, 2025</strong>.</p><p><strong>Applicable sellers:</strong> This policy applies to Sellers whose total number of products ordered within the month reaches at least 10 items.</p><h2 id="h_01K5BG9DX56BVCNCDBD3QB3F75">I. Cancellation Rate Regulations</h2><p>Oreka understands that the operation process may occasionally lead to unintended mistakes. Therefore, we have established a threshold cancellation rate to support Sellers. If this threshold is exceeded, the policy terms will be applied accordingly.</p><ul>
<li>
<strong>Allowed cancellation rate:</strong> up to 30% of the total number of products ordered within the reporting period (monthly).</li>
<li>
<strong>Condition:</strong> The policy only applies to orders canceled due to reasons originating from the Seller.</li>
</ul><h2 id="h_01K5BG9DX5SZARN536P5N0THA7">II. Policy When Exceeding the Allowed Cancellation Rate</h2><p>When a Sellerâ€™s cancellation rate exceeds 30%, both the operational handling fee and user warning display will be applied:</p><h3 id="h_01K5BG9DX5JY6V667JBW6D2G7E">1. Operational Handling Fee</h3><ul>
<li>
<span class="highlight">Fee: 10,000 VND</span> for each product canceled exceeding the allowed threshold.</li>
<li>Processing: This fee will be automatically deducted from the Seller's Oreka Wallet on the 5th day of the following month.</li>
</ul><h4 id="h_01K5BG9DX54PRG22ZVE440R8SG">Calculation Formula:</h4><ul>
<li>Accepted cancellations = [Total number of products ordered in the month] Ã— 30%</li>
<li>Penalized cancellations = [Total number of products canceled by the seller] â€“ [Accepted cancellations]</li>
<li>Total Operational Handling Fee = [Penalized cancellations] Ã— 10,000 VND</li>
<li><em>Note: The result of the percentage calculation will be rounded using standard mathematical rounding rules (â‰¥ 0.5 rounds up, &lt; 0.5 rounds down).</em></li>
</ul><div class="example">
<p><strong>Example:</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>Total products ordered = 101</li>
<li>Products canceled = 40</li>
<li>Accepted = 101 Ã— 30% = 30.3 â‰ˆ 30</li>
<li>Penalized = 40 â€“ 30 = 10</li>
<li>Total fee = 10 Ã— 10,000 = <strong>100,000 VND</strong>
</li>
</ul>
</div><h3 id="h_01K5BG9DX5HGVQHYEGTA70SJC5">2. Warning Display to Buyers</h3><p>Oreka will display a warning on product pages indicating that the Seller has a high order cancellation rate, in order to provide transparency to buyers.</p><figure class="wysiwyg-image"><img data-ck-upload-id="efeb20a3a79a4e7fef3093b676ec46947"></figure><h2 id="h_01K5BG9DX5GEC3GXKFDRW9A9G5">III. Recommendations to Improve Cancellation Rate</h2><p>To proactively manage performance and avoid unnecessary operational fees, Oreka recommends Sellers:</p><ul>
<li>Regularly audit and update inventory status.</li>
<li>Process incoming orders promptly.</li>
<li>Only list products that are confirmed to be in stock and ready for delivery.</li>
</ul><div class="contact">
<p>For any questions regarding this policy, please contact Orekaâ€™s Seller Support team for assistance:</p>
<p>ğŸ“ Hotline: <strong>090.4433.126</strong><br>ğŸ“§ Email: <a href="mailto:hotro@oreka.vn">hotro@oreka.vn</a></p>
</div><p><em>Thank you for partnering with Oreka.vn! ğŸ’š</em></p>

#### Invoice Policy Update on Oreka.vn Starting June 30, 2025

**ID:** 48313194857241 | **Votes:** 0 | **Updated:** 5/9/2025
**URL:** [https://oreka.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/48313194857241-Invoice-Policy-Update-on-Oreka-vn-Starting-June-30-2025](https://oreka.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/48313194857241-Invoice-Policy-Update-on-Oreka-vn-Starting-June-30-2025)

<div style="color: #333; font-family: Arial, sans-serif; line-height: 1.6;">
<p>To ensure <strong>accurate, transparent, and legally compliant invoice issuance</strong>, Oreka would like to inform all Sellers about our updated invoicing policy, effective from <strong>June 30, 2025</strong>, as follows:</p>
<h3 id="h_01JYNJYWYK71X1QVCST04EW7XS">
<br><strong>A. Eligible for Invoice Issuance</strong>
</h3>
<p>Oreka will <strong>only issue invoices</strong> to accounts that meet the <strong>valid verification requirements</strong>:</p>

</tr></thead>

<tr>

</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="border: 1px solid #ccc; padding: 8px;">Business</td>

</td>

</tbody>
</table></figure><h3 id="h_01JYNJYWYKH7A5M6QQPBC8EGG7">

<p>ğŸ‘‰ <strong>The system will automatically reject</strong> invoice issuance if the verification is not valid.</p>

<ol>
<li>Go to: <strong>[My Account] â†’ [Verify Information]</strong>
</li>

<li>
<strong>Citizen ID (CCCD)</strong> for individuals</li>
<li>
<strong>Tax Identification Number (TIN)</strong> for businesses</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
<p>ğŸ“Œ Please follow the instructions provided in the system interface.</p>
<h3 id="h_01JYNJYWYK21Q5EHKQGRJ1PRGQ">
<br>D. Important Notes</h3>
<ul>
<li>This policy <strong>applies to all Sellers</strong> on Oreka.vn.</li>
<li>
<strong>Starting June 30, 2025</strong>, only accounts with valid verification will be eligible for invoice issuance.</li>
<li>Even if a transaction is valid, <strong>invoices will not be issued</strong> without a valid CCCD or TIN.</li>
</ul>
<h3 id="h_01JYNJYWYKGP9R164AG1X3H5A2">

#### Seller Guidelines

**ID:** 900006900483 | **Votes:** 0 | **Updated:** 1/8/2024
**URL:** [https://oreka.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/900006900483-Seller-Guidelines](https://oreka.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/900006900483-Seller-Guidelines)

<p>Once the product has been successfully delivered, as soon as the Buyer reviews the product or after 3 days if there are no complaints, the order will be completed, the money will be transferred to your Oreka account.</p>
<p>Before that, you need to verify the identity of your Oreka account via ID card/ CCCD/ Passport if it is a personal account or Business Registration Certificate if it is a business account.</p>
<p>By following the instructions below for Sellers, Oreka will ensure the safety of the transaction:</p>
<p>* The listing item must be a legal item owned by the Seller<br>* The item being sold must not violate any regulations<br>* The item must not be on Oreka's Prohibited Items list<br>* If requested, the seller must transfer all rights or remove all restrictions on the goods at the time of purchase<br>* Buyers want to know what they are getting. Provide them with all the details. This will also maximize the chance of a sale. Details include:<br>- Size<br>- Brand<br>- Describe any defects or damage to the product<br>- Proof of authenticity<br>- Quantity<br>- Provide clear photos taken by you<br>Please do not use stock photos from websites<br>If there are any imperfections, please provide clear photos to avoid return requests<br>If listing multiple items, you must provide clear photos of each item<br>If you choose to ship yourself, please contact Oreka for instructions. Oreka will not be involved in the shipping process but will ensure the safety of the transaction for both Buyer and Seller.<br>Update the buyer regularly with progress<br>Seller must deliver the item to the carrier within 3 days of purchase.</p>

#### Tax withholding regulations for individual sellers

**ID:** 44743104293657 | **Votes:** 0 | **Updated:** 7/4/2025
**URL:** [https://oreka.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/44743104293657-Tax-withholding-regulations-for-individual-sellers](https://oreka.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/44743104293657-Tax-withholding-regulations-for-individual-sellers)

<p>Starting from April 1, 2025, according to the latest regulation issued by the Government of Vietnam regarding e-commerce platforms and individual/business sellers, OREKA will collect a 1.5% tax (including 1% Value Added Tax (VAT) and 0.5% Personal Income Tax) from applicable sellers and submit it to the government on their behalf.</p>
<p><strong>A. New Regulations from the Tax Management Law</strong></p>
<p>According to Law No. 56/2024/QH15 ("Law No. 56") issued by the National Assembly providing guidance on Tax Management, from April 1, 2025, e-commerce platforms (ECPs) are responsible for withholding, declaring, and paying taxes on behalf of individual business households and individual sellers operating on the platform.</p>
<p><strong>B. Oreka's Responsibilities</strong></p>
<p>Oreka is responsible for:</p>
<ul>
<li>Withholding, declaring the withheld tax, and paying tax on behalf of the Seller as required by regulations.</li>
<li>Providing relevant information to the Tax Authority (TA).</li>
<li>Assisting Sellers in fulfilling their tax obligations in compliance with current regulations.</li>
</ul>
<table style="border-collapse: collapse; width: 100%; background-color: #ffffff; border: 2px solid #000000;">
<tbody>
<tr style="background-color: #ffffff;">
<td style="width: 44.1905%; border: 2px solid #000000; padding: 4px;"><strong>Business Type</strong></td>
<td style="width: 30.0475%; border: 2px solid #000000; padding: 4px;"><strong>Tax Withholding, Declaration &amp; Payment</strong></td>
<td style="width: 25.7619%; border: 2px solid #000000; padding: 4px;"><strong>Information Provision</strong></td>
</tr>
<tr style="background-color: #ffffff;">
<td style="border: 2px solid #000000; padding: 4px;">Individual business households, individual sellers</td>
<td style="border: 2px solid #000000; padding: 4px;">NEWLY APPLIED</td>
<td style="border: 2px solid #000000; padding: 4px;">APPLIED</td>
</tr>
<tr style="background-color: #ffffff;">
<td style="border: 2px solid #000000; padding: 4px;">Organizations (LLC, Joint Stock Companies, Partnerships, Private Enterprises, etc.)</td>
<td style="border: 2px solid #000000; padding: 4px;">NOT APPLIED</td>
<td style="border: 2px solid #000000; padding: 4px;">APPLIED</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p>Â </p>
<p>Oreka is currently working closely with the TA and making necessary preparations to comply with the new regulations. We will provide detailed guidance on applicable tax rates and tax calculation methods as soon as an official Decree is issued by the Government.</p>
<p><strong>C. Seller's Responsibilities</strong></p>
<p>According to Law No. 56, Decree 52/2013/ND-CP on E-commerce, and Decree 91/2022/ND-CP, Sellers have the following obligations:</p>
<p>1. For Sellers who are Organizations (LLC, Joint Stock Companies, Partnerships, Private Enterprises, etc.)</p>
<ul>
<li>No changes are applied, and the system does not withhold tax on the Seller's transactions.</li>
</ul>
<p>2. For Sellers who are Individual Business Households, Individual Sellers</p>
<ul>
<li>Sellers can still list products and process orders as usual.</li>
<li>Provide complete and accurate information, including business type, full name, tax identification number (TIN), and identification details, so that Oreka can fulfill tax obligations.</li>
<li>Regularly check and update business information on the platform.</li>
<li>Note: The displayed price in the Listing and Order sections already includes tax.</li>
<li>1.5% Tax will only be withheld after the order is completed.</li>
<li>Sellers can view detailed tax deductions in the "My Money" section.</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>D. Important Notes</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>If an individual business household or individual seller does not provide complete information, Oreka will still withhold tax on revenue-generating transactions from April 1, 2025.</li>
<li>Withheld tax amounts will not be refunded if the Seller provides incorrect business type information.</li>
<li>Sellers can download Revenue Reports from the Oreka system based on the information they provide.</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>E. Other Important Information</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>Sellers must ensure proper business registration, tax registration, and information updates on the platform.</li>
<li>According to the guidance from the General Department of Taxation at https://canhantmdt.gdt.gov.vn, individual business households and individual sellers can register for a TIN ending in 888 to facilitate tax declaration and payment for online businesses.</li>
<li>Before the new regulations take effect, Sellers must still declare and pay taxes under the current rules.</li>
<li>âš ï¸ Note: The withholding, declaration, and tax payment on behalf of Sellers do not exempt them from their tax finalization obligations with the tax authorities.</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>F. Fraud Prevention</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>Sellers should keep their electronic tax account (eTax Mobile) secure and not share passwords or OTPs with anyone.</li>
<li>Oreka will never request Sellers to provide login information for tax compliance purposes.</li>
<li>If there are any concerns, Sellers should contact the Tax Authority directly or seek advice from reputable tax consultants.</li>
</ul>
<p>ğŸ“Œ For any inquiries, please contact Oreka's Customer Support at 090.4433.126</p>

---

#### The overall transaction

**ID:** 900006620083 | **Votes:** 0 | **Updated:** 7/4/2025
**URL:** [https://oreka.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/900006620083-The-overall-transaction](https://oreka.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/900006620083-The-overall-transaction)

<p>1. When the item is ordered, the Seller will receive a notification from Oreka via app/email about the new order. The Seller has 72 hours to confirm the order with Oreka.</p>
<p>2. After the order has been confirmed, the Seller has 3 days (72 hours) to ship the order by having the shipping unit come to the address you registered to pick up the order or the Seller will send the order to the post office.</p>
<p>3. After the order is successfully delivered, the Buyer will have 3 days to check the product.</p>
<p>4. After 3 days, if there are no complaints from the Buyer, Oreka will record the successful transaction and the sales proceeds will be added to the Seller's Oreka account. The Seller can withdraw money to his/her own bank account after successfully verifying his/her identity.</p>
<p>Â </p>

---

#### Trust & safety

**ID:** 900005675786 | **Votes:** 0 | **Updated:** 7/4/2025
**URL:** [https://oreka.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/900005675786-Trust-safety](https://oreka.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/900005675786-Trust-safety)

<p><span data-sheets-value='{"1":2,"2":"Oreka guarantees payment for your sales. Buyer pays for your item, before you even ship the item. Oreka holds this payment from buyer on your behalf. After you ship the item to buyer, buyer has 3 days to confirm that the shipped item matches the description mentioned at Oreka. As long as your shipped item matches the description you mentioned at Oreka, we guarantee you payment for your sales."}' data-sheets-userformat='{"2":897,"3":{"1":0},"10":1,"11":4,"12":0}'>Oreka commits to pay the Seller in full for the transaction.<br>Oreka will temporarily hold the amount that the Buyer has paid for the item during the transaction.<br>After 3 days, if there is no complaint from the Buyer, Oreka will record the transaction as successful and the sales proceeds will be added to the Seller's Oreka account.</span></p>
<p>Â </p>
<p>Â </p>

#### Ways to "Give" on Oreka

**ID:** 20501567730073 | **Votes:** 0 | **Updated:** 7/4/2025
**URL:** [https://oreka.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/20501567730073-Ways-to-Give-on-Oreka](https://oreka.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/20501567730073-Ways-to-Give-on-Oreka)

<p>Giving is an act of eternal meaning and preserving precious values â€‹â€‹for life. The giver can choose one of the two ways below.</p>
<p>- Method 1: Give your old items in the "Free Items" category and the recipient will pay the shipping fee<br>- Method 2: Set a low price and free shipping (Seller pays the shipping fee) for the recipient</p>
<p>Thank you for spreading Oreka's environmental protection message through the act of "giving".</p>

<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">Báº±ng cÃ¡ch Ä‘á»“ng Ã½ vá»›i cÃ¡c Äiá»u khoáº£n nÃ y, báº¡n cho phÃ©p Oreka vÃ / hoáº·c há»‡ thá»‘ng xá»­ lÃ½ thanh toÃ¡n cá»§a Oreka tÃ­nh phÃ­ hoáº·c ghi ná»£ cho PhÆ°Æ¡ng tiá»‡n thanh toÃ¡n Ä‘Æ°á»£c chá»‰ Ä‘á»‹nh cá»§a báº¡n (náº¿u cÃ³) khi báº¡n thá»±c hiá»‡n cÃ¡c giao dá»‹ch hoáº·c náº¿u báº¡n pháº£i tráº£ thÃªm phÃ­ hoáº·c sá»‘ tiá»n mÃ  Oreka dÃ nh cho (cÃ¡c) Dá»‹ch vá»¥.Â </span></p>

<h3 id="h_01HEPG84M0556V1W1ZAAJVZ9WK"><strong>13. Viá»‡c há»§y giao dá»‹ch, hoÃ n tiá»n</strong></h3>

<h3 id="h_01HEPG84M1NQPZSKB0F21J58CY"><strong>19. Bá»“i thÆ°á»ng, Giá»›i háº¡n trÃ¡ch nhiá»‡m phÃ¡p lÃ½</strong></h3>
